Explanations: (C) -Chain (R)- Repeating (N)- normal command block
A - Always active No-Needs redstone CO- conditional

1. R A /effect @e[name=Worm] minecraft:speed 1 3
2. C A /execute @e[name=Worm] ~ ~ ~ summon Spider ~ ~ ~ {Silent:1b,CustomName:Vold,DropItems:0b}
3. C A /execute @e[name=Vold] ~ ~ ~ /kill @e[type=Item,r=10]
4. C A /kill @e[name=Vold]

Photographer: (needs a carrot on a stick)
Init command: /scoreboard objectives add repa stat.useItem.minecraft.carrot_on_a_stick
1. R A /scoreboard players tag @a[score_repa_min=1] add repa1 {SelectedItem:{Damage:0s}}
2. C A /scoreboard players tag @a[score_repa_min=1] add repa2 {SelectedItem:{Damage:1s}}
3. C A /execute @a[tag=repa2] ~ ~ ~ playsound minecraft:entity.armorstand.break master @a ~ ~ ~ 1000 2.0
4. C A /execute @a[tag=repa2] ~ ~ ~ effect @a night_vision 1 1
5. C A Co /effect @a minecraft:slowness 1 5
6. C A /scoreboard players tag @a remove repa2
7. C A Co /effect @a minecraft:blindness 1 1
8. C A Co /execute @a ~ ~ ~ effect @e[r=2,type=!Player] wither 10 5
9. C A Co /effect @a minecraft:slowness 1 5
10. C A /scoreboard players set @a repa 0

Fire eggs:
1. R A /execute @e[type=ThrownEgg] ~ ~ ~ /entitydata @e[r=5] {Fire:100}
2. C A /execute @e[type=ThrownEgg] ~ ~ ~ /particle lava ~ ~ ~ 0.1 0.1 0.1 0.1 100

Alien maker: (Name a wither_skeleton "Allien", sorry for typo)
1. R A /execute @e[name=Allien] ~ ~1 ~ /particle smoke ~ ~ ~ 0.1 0.1 0.1 0.1 100 normal @a
2. C A /effect @e[name=Allien] minecraft:invisibility 1 1
3. C A /execute @e[name=Allien] ~ ~ ~ /effect @e[r=4,type=!Skeleton] 15 1 5
4. C A /execute @e[name=Allien] ~ ~ ~ /playsound minecraft:entity.endermen.hurt voice @a ~ ~10 ~ 1 0.0

Ghoul: (Name a bat "Bloody")
1. R A /execute @e[name=Bloody] ~ ~ ~ /particle blockcrack ~ ~ ~ 0.1 0 0 0 10 normal @a 152
2. C A /effect @e[name=Bloody] minecraft:invisibility 1 1
3. C A /execute @e[name=Bloody] ~ ~ ~ /effect @e[r=3] minecraft:wither 1 10
4. C A /entitydata @e[name=Bloody] {Silent:1b}

Instakill Bow:
Init command: /scoreboard objectives add inGround dummy inGround
1. R A execute @e[type=Arrow] ~ ~ ~ scoreboard players set @e[c=1,r=0,type=Arrow] inGround 1 {inGround:1b}
2. C A execute @e[type=Arrow] ~ ~ ~ particle reddust ~ ~ ~ 0 0 0 0.1 30 force @e 152
3. C A execute @e[type=Arrow,score_inGround_min=1] ~ ~ ~ /playsound minecraft:entity.guardian.death master @e ~ ~ ~ 1000 
4. C A execute @e[type=Arrow,score_inGround_min=1] ~ ~ ~ /kill @e[r=3]
5. C A kill @e[type=Arrow,score_inGround_min=1]
